p. 1

अ, The first letter of the Devanāgarī alphabet, pronounced as u in up or o in come; a privative or negative inseparable particle like in or un in English words, as अकारण. When prefixed to words beginning with a vowel, it is followed by न, for the sake of euphony, as अनादि. An interjection expressive of pity.
अऊत, m. a man who dies without issue, an unmarried man, a blockhead.
